msg:Location:
Heart of Beijing, big shopping malls by walking distance, lots of restaurants inside the modern malls and not expensive at all.
Giant supermarket "Fresh Hippo" next to the hotel, 24hrs convenience store less than 1 min walk, so no worry about your night snacks and drinks.

Breakfast:
Lots of variety of foods, taste is good and up to standard. 
My compliments to the coffee guy (Mr Nice guy) and waffle lady (helpful), egg counter chef (he can understand English), sorry I forget to ask their names ＞o＜.

Front desk:
Check-in is fast and check out is hassle free. My kids got a bear dolls from Amy Tao when I check out, Thanks.

Room:
I changed my room after 1st night becos something broken and need to be fixed, after that no complain. Big TV comes with lots of local channels, Nat Geo, MTV, HBO, etc. Big bathtub, nice bed, big room and comfy bed, up to standard.

Overall:
Value for Money and up to standard.

When I arrived, I entered the lobby with a light scent. It's tangy, worthy of being a long-established five-star hotel, and the lobby is spacious and grand! The decoration is full of Chinese New Year flavor! 👍
The front desk staff gave a warm welcome. There was a light aroma when entering the room. The bedding was clean and comfortable. The bathroom was separated from wet and dry and had a bathtub🛁. The most surprising thing was that when I returned from shopping in Sanlitun on New Year's Eve the next day, the room was cleaned up by the cleaning lady on the 20th floor. The hotel is clean and comfortable. Knowing that we live in the south and are worried about the dryness, we put 6 bottles of water for us. The last Easter egg was: when we were about to check out, the staff gave us a New Year gift. What a surprise🥰🥰

msg:On New Year's Eve, as long as you don't go out of Beijing to celebrate the New Year, you are used to staying in a hotel.
On New Year's Eve, spend a night in a different environment, relaxed and comfortable, and for those who are keen on staying in hotels, there is a sense of happiness.
First of all, I would like to thank the telephone service lady of Wanda Vista Hotel for calling early, asking about the personal requirements for staying in the hotel, helping to upgrade the high-floor room, and enthusiastically explaining the parking problem in advance. When I opened the door of the hotel at night, I was very satisfied and pleasantly surprised. Thank you for this lady with a nice voice. It’s just a sequela of Yangkang. I forgot to ask her name before and after staying in the hotel.

Facilities: A standard five-star hotel, indicating that it needs to face the location of the third ring road. On New Year's Eve, the high-rise buildings are brightly lit. The big bed is comfortable, and the water flow in the bathroom is adjusted to the maximum, which can be called a water shock massage. Unfortunately, there is no capsule coffee machine

Service: Read the reviews and praise the service. The lady with a nice voice really warmed me up before I checked in. Thank you for arranging it on the 20th floor, where you can watch the colorful lights on Beijing New Year's Eve. In fact, I have always been used to staying at the China World Hotel on New Year’s Eve, but I almost never answered warm calls before check-in. Especially last year’s New Year’s Eve, because of the location of the room, the service attitude of the short-haired and fat front desk lady made me hesitate for a long time when I made a reservation this year. Fortunately, Mr. Wei secretly suggested that he chose Wanda Vista.

Hygiene: Sanitary facilities are good, especially when the water flow in the bathroom is adjusted to the maximum, it can be called a water jet massage

Environment: Located in the CBD circle, the price is the most suitable among many hotels. As a senior hotel person, the price/performance ratio is absolutely super value. There is free parking at the entrance of the hotel, and the underground charges are charged on time. This is also a rare convenience in nearby hotels.

The first cup of coffee in the Year of the Rabbit, in the warm sunshine of Mandarin Hotel. Oh, the little brother at the front desk gave a free breakfast, and the services from room service to the breakfast manager were all highly praised. Star standard breakfast, food quality control is excellent. And this cup of latte has reached the high standard of a cafe. The breakfast time is from 7:00 to 11:00, which is too humane for people who are lazy.

Here, I spent a wonderful New Year's Eve, a good mood, and I believe that everything will get better and better!

msg:從進門開始，無論走到哪裡，衹要遇到酒店服務員，都會熱情地問好。如果有任何需求，也會很快回應，送到房間的速度非常快。酒店有豪華房、行政房、豪華套房，除此之外，還有海底小縱隊的主題房，孩子們一定喜歡這樣的主題房呢!客房的設計大方亮麗。通透的房間設計、皮革桌面書枱、LED護眼燈，浴缸前方還有電視，在泡湯的同時還可以刷劇，簡直太貼心了!
當然，最讓人眼前一亮的則是無敵的窗外景觀了!夜幕降臨，坐在窗邊的沙發上，盡情的去欣賞窗外的美景吧!在房間裏可以看到長安街上來來往往的車輛，國貿商城以及CBD核心區的辦公樓，當然還有代表性建築“中國尊”。如此核心的位置，交通便利、購物餐飲下樓就達的寶藏酒店我太愛啦!
萬達作為大品牌，在細節方面也做到了淋漓盡致。床上有大號和小號枕頭，可以根據自己的喜好進行選擇。累了一天，躺在軟硬適中的床上，睡個安穩覺，比什麼都重要。
酒店裡的配套也非常齊全。足不出户就可以選擇不同的餐廳:川菜、粵菜、淮揚菜、西餐、日料..累了可以選擇去做個SPA放鬆一下，還有美髮中心、KTV。當然了，愛健身的我怎麼能錯過健身房呢!健身房乾淨整潔，設施齊全，還有瑜伽室可以使用。一邊跑步一邊欣賞窗外的夜景，感覺眼睛被治癒了。
無論是商務出差還是來旅遊度假，萬達文華都是一個很好的選擇呢!

msg:最近來北京第二次住這個酒店了。
首先，交通便利，打車或者地鐵（近地鐵一號線）非常方便。
其次，房間很乾凈，雖然裝修有點時間了，但是整體很整潔。
住這個酒店最主要的是，服務特別好，特人性化。我出差住酒店主要選入住舒適，服務周到。其中，上一次入住，大堂喇經理幫忙升級房型，人性周到服務讓人記憶深刻。這一次，因為晚上7點火車，酒店大堂經理（不太禮貌，這次沒有注意到姓名），考慮到火車情況，她主動幫忙延遲退房，這樣人性化的體貼關心比某些酒店的口號更能打動消費者。
還會選擇入住！
